The environment of the hotel is very good, the service is very warm, the hot springs are very large and there are many pools, and there are many places for children to play. The steam room on the second floor is also very comfortable, with both high and low temperatures. The buffet steak at noon is very professional, very tender, and not at all. Not firewood. There are also water slides and many small animals outside, which children especially like. All in all, I highly recommend everyone to play. In particular, I would like to thank Ma Mengke in the hotel lobby. Seeing that we were bringing children, we even upgraded the parent-child room. The service is very enthusiastic. I plan to contact her directly next time I make a reservation.
